***командовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:командовать.html>кома́ндовать</a> (2714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:командовать.html>кома́ндовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">komándovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скомандовать.html>скома́ндовать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to command, to give orders (+ instrumental case)</li>
<li>to be in command (of) (+ instrumental case)</li>
<li>to boss around, to order around, to dictate (+ instrumental case)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:командор.html>командо́р</a> (17519)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:командор.html>командо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">komandór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:командор.html>командо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:командор.html>командо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:командор.html>командо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>knight commander, commander; commodore</li></ol>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:переносной.html>переносно́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a>">перен.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:разговорный.html>разгово́рное</a>">разг.</span> распоряжающийся, приказывающий <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Этот человек со всеми вёл себя одинаково: он, видимо, говорил всё, что хотел сказать, и всё, что он говорил, звучало убедительно, во всём чувствовалось отношение к людям властное, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">командующее</span>, но доброе, дружелюбное. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Очень хороша Гонзикова ― О. Викландт, энергично <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">командующая</span> всеми действиями, развертывающимися то на кухне, возле раскаленной плиты, то на площадке для танцев, где кипит пестрый народный праздник веселых и трудолюбивых людей новой Чехии. </span></li>
</ul></li>


</ol>

<ol><li>приказывающий</li>
<li>распоряжающийся, приказывающий</li>
</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a> (4534)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*komarъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">komár</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>комара́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>комары́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>комаро́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mosquito
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>но́са</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> подто́чит (the mosquito won’t sharpen its nose)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>komár</b> nósa ne podtóčit (the mosquito won’t sharpen its nose)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">impeccably done!</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">маляри́йный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">maljaríjnyj <b>komár</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">malaria mosquito</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">кровососу́щий <b><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krovososúščij <b>komár</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">bloodsucking mosquito</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">пятиполо́сный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pjatipolósnyj <b>komár</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Culex_quinquefasciatus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Culex quinquefasciatus"><i>Culex quinquefasciatus</i></a></span>) <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/southern_house_mosquito" class="extiw" title="w:southern house mosquito">southern house mosquito</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обыкновенный.html>обыкнове́нный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obyknovénnyj <b>komár</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Culex_pipiens" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Culex pipiens"><i>Culex pipiens</i></a></span>) <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/northern_house_mosquito" class="extiw" title="w:northern house mosquito">northern house mosquito</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">маляри́йный четырёхточечный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">maljaríjnyj četyrjóxtočečnyj <b>komár</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Anopheles_quadrimaculatus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Anopheles quadrimaculatus"><i>Anopheles quadrimaculatus</i></a></span>) common malaria mosquito</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">маляри́йный <a href = vnd.unilang:обыкновенный.html>обыкнове́нный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">maljaríjnyj obyknovénnyj <b>komár</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Anopheles_maculipennis" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Anopheles maculipennis"><i>Anopheles maculipennis</i></a></span>) <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/spotted-wing_mosquito" class="extiw" title="w:spotted-wing mosquito">spotted-wing mosquito</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болотный.html>боло́тный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:коричневый.html>кори́чневый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bolótnyj koríčnevyj <b>komár</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Aedes_cantator" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Aedes cantator"><i>Aedes cantator</i></a></span>) <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/brown_salt-marsh_mosquito" class="extiw" title="w:brown salt-marsh mosquito">brown salt-marsh mosquito</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болотный.html>боло́тный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:калифорнийский.html>калифорни́йский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bolótnyj kaliforníjskij <b>komár</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Aedes_squamiger" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Aedes squamiger"><i>Aedes squamiger</i></a></span>) <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/California_salt-marsh_mosquito" class="extiw" title="w:California salt-marsh mosquito">California salt-marsh mosquito</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">желтолихора́дочный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">želtolixorádočnyj <b>komár</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>Aedes aegypti</i>) <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/tiger_yellow-fever_mosquito" class="extiw" title="w:tiger yellow-fever mosquito">tiger yellow-fever mosquito</a></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бескрылый.html>бескры́лый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">beskrýlyj <b>komár</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Chionea" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Chionea"><i>Chionea</i></a></span>) <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/snow_fly" class="extiw" title="w:snow fly">snow fly</a></span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>gnat</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mechanics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hollow punch, punch press</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metallurgy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nibbling machine, blank-cutting machine</li></ol>

***комариный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:комариный.html>комари́ный</a> (18109)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комар.html>кома́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">komár</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ínyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комариный.html>комари́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">komarínyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mosquito</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***комбайн.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:комбайн.html>комба́йн</a> (12648)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">combine</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комбайн.html>комба́йн</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kombájn</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комбайн.html>комба́йна</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комбайн.html>комба́йны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комбайн.html>комба́йнов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> food processor, processor</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mining</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> coal cutter-loader, coal-plough machine</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">agriculture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> combine, combine harvester, harvester, picker</li></ol>

<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:командир.html>команди́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:батальон.html>батальо́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">komandír batalʹóna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:командир.html>команди́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:батарея.html>батаре́и</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">komandír bataréi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***комбинация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:комбинация.html>комбина́ция</a> (7416)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комбинация.html>комбина́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kombinácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комбинация.html>комбина́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комбинация.html>комбина́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комбинация.html>комбина́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>combination</li>
<li>scheme, system</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports<span class="ib-comma">,</span> politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> manoeuvre</li>
<li>slip (women’s undergarment)</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комендант.html>коменда́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">komendánt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комендант.html>коменда́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комендант.html>коменда́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комендант.html>коменда́нтов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">коменда́нтша</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:комиссариат.html>комиссариа́т</a> (25687)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комиссариат.html>комиссариа́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">komissariát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комиссариат.html>комиссариа́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комиссариат.html>комиссариа́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комиссариат.html>комиссариа́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>commissariat (any public administrative agency headed by a commissar, <a href = vnd.unilang:комиссар.html>комисса́р</a>)</li></ol>

***комиссионка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:комиссионка.html>комиссио́нка</a> (23806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">комиссио́н(ный)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">komissión(nyj)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from an ellipsis of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комиссионный.html>комиссио́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:магазин.html>магази́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">komissiónnyj magazín</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">commission store</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комиссионка.html>комиссио́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">komissiónka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комиссионка.html>комиссио́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комиссионка.html>комиссио́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комиссионка.html>комиссио́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> commission shop <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">type of secondhand store where people who sell goods to the store receive no money until the item is bought, at which point the store owner takes a commission</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">комиссионе́р</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">komissionér</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">комиссионе́рский</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">komissionérskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">комиссионе́рство</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">komissionérstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">комиссионе́рствовать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">komissionérstvovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***комиссия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:комиссия.html>коми́ссия</a> (1504)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">commissio</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комиссия.html>коми́ссия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">komíssija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комиссия.html>коми́ссии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комиссия.html>коми́ссии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комиссия.html>коми́ссий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>chores</li>
<li>commission, committee</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комитет.html>комите́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">komitét</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комитет.html>комите́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комитет.html>комите́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комитет.html>комите́тов</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комок.html>комо́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">komók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-atʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***комментировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:комментировать.html>комменти́ровать</a> (9005)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kommentieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комментировать.html>комменти́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kommentírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокомментировать.html>прокомменти́ровать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">закомменти́ровать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to comment <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">various senses</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокомментировать.html>прокомменти́ровать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prokommentírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to comment, to comment out (computer code)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">закомменти́ровать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zakommentírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комментарий.html>коммента́рий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">davátʹ kommentárij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
